================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;

			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_F-150/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP F-150 → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	if enabled then
		local rotLights = ELSModel.RotLights;
		for i, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end;
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;

end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:35
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_G_Wagon/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP G Wagon → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]

local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--Lightbar
	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);


if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do			
					F1(0);
					F2(1);
					wait(0.3)						

					F1(1);
					F2(0);
					wait(0.3)	
				end
			end)
		end)()	
		
	else
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_G_Wagon/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

				if colour then

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_G_Wagon/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_G_Wagon/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe
    Parent: CFMP Tahoe
    Properties:

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local F9 = elsModule(ELSModel.F9);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3);
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4);
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5);
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6);
	local G7 = elsModule(ELSModel.G7);
	local G8 = elsModule(ELSModel.G8);
	local G9 = elsModule(ELSModel.G9);
	local K1 = elsModule(ELSModel.K1);
	local K2 = elsModule(ELSModel.K2);
	local K3 = elsModule(ELSModel.K3);
	local K4 = elsModule(ELSModel.K4);
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4);
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1);
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2);
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3);
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4);
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local E1 = elsModule(ELSModel.E1);
	local E2 = elsModule(ELSModel.E2);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					F8(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					F9(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.09)
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					F8(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					F9(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.09)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G7(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G8(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G9(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.09);
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G7(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G8(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					G9(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.09);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do

					F7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));

		F7(1)

		G4(1) 
		G5(1)

	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
					R1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.04);
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		F9(1)

		R3(1)

	end
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/CFMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → CFMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/1MPR/Defence_Truck/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → Defence Truck → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	if enabled then
		local rotLights = ELSModel.RotLights;
		for i, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end;
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → 1MPR → Defence Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Allied_Forces/CAF_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Allied Forces → CAF G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Allied_Forces/CAF_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Allied Forces → CAF G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Allied_Forces/CAF_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Allied Forces → CAF G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7)
	
	--Side lights

	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2)
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3)
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4)
	
	--Rear lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)	
	
	if enabled then

				F4(1);
				F5(1);
				F6(1);

		coroutine.wrap(function()

				S1(1);
				S3(1);

				S1(0);
				S2(0);					
				S3(1);
				S4(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
					
				S1(1);
				S2(1);					
				S3(0);
				S4(0);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
					
				S1(1);
				S2(1);					
				S3(0);
				S4(0);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do						
				R1(0);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(0);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)						
					
				R1(0);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(0);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)					
					
				R1(1);
				R2(0);		
				R3(0);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);

				R4(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/ALSU_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → ALSU Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/ALSU_Ambulance/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → ALSU Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/ALSU_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → ALSU Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/ALSU_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → ALSU Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;

		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/BCAS_Ambulance/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → BCAS Ambulance → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5)
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6)
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7)
	
	--Side lights
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1)
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2)
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3)
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4)
	
	--Rear lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)	
	
	if enabled then	
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do	
				F1(1);
				F2(1);
				F3(1);
				F4(1);
				F5(1);
				F6(1);
				F7(1);						
				wait()													
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do		
				S1(0);
				S2(0);					
				S3(1);
				S4(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)		
					
				S1(0);
				S2(0);					
				S3(1);
				S4(1);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
					
				S1(1);
				S2(1);					
				S3(0);
				S4(0);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
					
				S1(1);
				S2(1);					
				S3(0);
				S4(0);				
				wait(0.15)						
					
				S1(1);
				S3(1);					
				wait(0.02)						
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do						
				R1(0);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(0);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)						
					
				R1(0);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(0);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)					
					
				R1(1);
				R2(0);		
				R3(0);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)					
					
				R1(1);
				R2(0);		
				R3(0);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.15)						
					
				R1(1);
				R2(1);		
				R3(1);
				R4(1);						
				wait(0.02)						
				end
			end)
		end)()			
		
		
	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)	
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		S1(1)
		S2(1)
		S3(1)
		S4(1)	
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/BCAS_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → BCAS Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/BCAS_Ambulance/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → BCAS Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/BCAS_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → BCAS Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/Ambulance/BCAS_Ambulance/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → Ambulance → BCAS Ambulance → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local LS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS1);
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3);
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4);
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5);
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6);
	local G7 = elsModule(ELSModel.G7);
	local G8 = elsModule(ELSModel.G8);
	local RS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS1);
	local K1 = elsModule(ELSModel.K1);
	local K2 = elsModule(ELSModel.K2);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09)
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09)
					G1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09)
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					LS1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					RS1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
